local po,ts = game:WaitForChild("CoreGui"):WaitForChild("RobloxPromptGui"):WaitForChild("promptOverlay"),game:GetService('TeleportService')
po.ChildAdded:connect(function(a)
if a.Name == 'ErrorPrompt' then

while task.wait(5) do pcall(function()
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(game:HttpGetAsync("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100")).data) do
if type(v) == "table" and v.id ~= game.JobId then
game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, v.id)
end 
end 
end) 
end

end
end)

repeat wait() until game:IsLoaded()
game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = "Wave Hub";Text = "Loading";Duration = 25;})
